    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              ITSS provides multi-vendor and brand independent IT services and solutions to its more than 100 customers which are leading companies in their sectors whole over Turkey. 

More than 80% of our employees are technical experts who have more than 15 years average  experience in their fields. Our HQ is in İstanbul and we have branch offices in Ankara, İzmir and Adana.

Our main focus is providing 7x24 contractual hw&amp;sw maintenance services to entry level, midrange and enterprise RISC, Sparc, x86 servers, storage systems, tape libraries, line printers and operating systems including AIX, System i, Solaris, Linux and Windows. As well as our contractual maintenance services, we also provide on-demand onsite repair and IMAC-D services to our customers. 

Our multi-vendor and brand independent identity makes us also the trusted advisor and solution provider of our customers who wants to renew or tranform their IT infrastructure. Also, it is our expertise to make cost efficient hardware upgrades to our customers exisiting infrastructures.
          </p>

          <dl class="mt-6">
              
    <div class="mb-2 flex papabear:mr-3 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:flex-wrap" data-test-id="about-us__website">
      <dt class="font-sans text-md font-bold text-color-text break-words w-40 papabear:flex-shrink-0 papabear:mr-3 mamabear:flex-shrink-0 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:mb-1">
          Web Sitesi
      </dt>
      <dd class="font-sans px-0.25 text-md text-color-text break-words overflow-hidden">

      http://www.itss.com.tr
      <icon class="align-middle" data-delayed-url="https://static.licdn.com/aero-v1/sc/h/49229g4q0jsla5l1xojq1wob9" aria-hidden="true"></icon>
    </a>
  
                  <p class="hidden" id="websiteLinkDescription">ITSS Bilişim Hizmetleri  için harici link</p>
                
      </dd>
    </div>
  
              
    <div class="mb-2 flex papabear:mr-3 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:flex-wrap" data-test-id="about-us__industry">
      <dt class="font-sans text-md font-bold text-color-text break-words w-40 papabear:flex-shrink-0 papabear:mr-3 mamabear:flex-shrink-0 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:mb-1">
